,," - write personal messages/requests to FB groups/persons who speaking languages, that are not yet translated here.
 - (for main doc. editor) categorize raws by topic before print
 - (for main doc. editor) File/ Email collaborators - ask them to finish untranslated/new texts
 - (for main doc. editor) Icons could be the first raw. It is easier to find a topic using visual search instead of reading all the text to find what you need.
 - (for main doc. editor) Split width of table in half. Print one half on front of A3 landscape paper, the other half on the back. Icons and ""Your countrie's language"" column could repeat on both sides.
 - (for main doc. editor) before printing select all text than from the menu bar press ""Text Wrapping/ Wrap"" to be sure that text won't be clipped, and not fully visible
